10)</li>\n<li>Click \"JazzCash\" → complete payment on JazzCash's page</li>\n<li>You should be redirected back to <code>/?payment=success</code></li>\n<li>The submission should auto-confirm (no admin 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"><path d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1
